## DECISION (576)
KEY                                                                 TIER   N  IN  DATE        MESSAGE
architecture/loop-as-runtime                                        high   1  19  2026-03-25  The vertex was always a loop. Loop becomes the first-class runtime: source, fold, boundary, tick. Vertex reduces to a named convergence loop with a store — the point where loops meet. Current 'loop' declarations in .vertex files are fold specs per kind, not loops. An actual loop is an attention circuit: multiple kinds, shared rhythm, one boundary. The inversion: vertex absorbed loop behavior because it IS a loop but was the only runtime, so every new attention circuit required a new vertex. This created vertex nesting, emit-by-vertex, vertex-scoping — all compensating for the missing loop primitive. Routing becomes vertex→loop→kind→key. Supersedes vertex-as-complete-contract, emit-by-vertex, vertex nesting, discover/combine, source-aware-aggregation. Rediscovery of Jan 27-30 design that was correctly deferred then — practical pressure now demands it.
design/three-layer-auth-composition                                 high   3  15  2026-05-16  REFINED 2026-05-16 (third position, recast from WIRE/SUBSTRATE/BODY to ATTESTATION/SUBSTRATE/BODY after local-case-as-primitive walk): three universal layers, none transport-specific. (1) ATTESTATION — every fact carries signature (Fact.signature); receive verifies against observer's Peer.key. Two sub-paths inside attestation: direct-trust (Peer.key pre-registered, local + known-peer) and federated-trust (vouch credential bridges, per-fact validation for non-local observers). (2) SUBSTRATE — vertex Peer/Grant filters fact-kind by observer (unchanged). (3) BODY — provenance chain (act=alice etc.) in payload, answers 'who is the human ultimately responsible.' OPEN: BODY's role vs Fact.signature semantics — signature-proves-emission vs signature-proves-responsibility — needs picking in owed session (thread/vouch-substrate-session-owed). CORRECTION FROM PRIOR VERSION (REFINED ×2): WIRE layer was over-fit on remote case. Local case is the primitive; signing/verification are universal; vouch is conditional inside attestation, not its own layer. Atoms evolve (Fact.signature, Peer.key); policy adoption progressive per design/attestation-substrate-with-progressive-policy.
design/attestation-substrate-with-progressive-policy                high   1  15  2026-05-16  Verdict 2026-05-16: Fact.signature and Peer.key evolve as STRUCTURAL atom fields (substrate change, one-time); verification policy is per-vertex PROGRESSIVE (strict/lenient/legacy-accept). Chosen from axis between config-default (atoms unchanged, sign+verify opt-in feature) and substrate-mandate (atoms structural, sign+verify mandatory, full design session owed first). Rationale: atoms move once → homogeneous ledger from transition point → 'lineage is structural' becomes true not aspirational. Verification adoption stays progressive at consumer layer → no big-bang migration → fits project's progressive-capability development pattern. Sign-on-emit is the default (with explicit escape hatches for internal/derived/legacy). Vouch is the federation path inside attestation, runs per-fact for observers not in local Peer registry (credential expiration checked each time, NOT cached as a Peer entry). Five open questions (vertex identity, tick-signing, BODY's role under universal sig, bootstrap order, escape-hatch policy) plus lib-boundary plus Peer-on-fact nag are owed but not immediate — surface as we hit them. See thread/vouch-substrate-session-owed. Caught: distributed-design-conversation is the failure mode of pure config-default (same questions re-derived per-adoption, answers drift); concentrated-upfront-session is the cost of pure substrate-mandate; option B splits the cost — substrate change concentrated, policy progressive.

design/lens-is-the-interface                                        high   2  11  2026-03-24  REFINED: 'Never load without a lens' becomes 'never load without an operation.' The operation IS the lens — it specifies the view (kind selection, projection, grouping, fidelity, format). The insight holds: raw fold is not the interface. But 'lens' now means three things: operation config (declarative, 80%), transform (Python, structured data out, 20%), and format protocol (renders to terminal/JSON/HTML/plain). The word 'lens' is user-facing shorthand for the full pipeline.
design/derived-keys-as-focus-filter                                 high   2  11  2026-04-24  Pattern: a derived view (ref graph, tick window, search, tag selection) yields a bounded key set; that key set filters or marks another view by membership. Known instances: (1) --refs pulls referenced (kind, key) pairs back into FoldState as focus — outbound/inbound refs are a key set, membership filters the target view. (2) TickWindow.added_keys / updated_keys are per-kind tuples of keys touched since prior boundary; they salience-mark items in the accumulated state. General shape: derived_view → key_set → filter(target_view). Captured before the third instance lands. Dissolves ad-hoc 'which items are relevant to X' queries. Composition property: key sets union cleanly (refs ∪ window-deltas) and intersect for narrow focus.
rendering/salience-driven-display                                   high   1  12  2026-04-26  Composes the verbosity-fidelity-review observed strain with cite-as-partial-information-primitives gripping-hand framing into a unified rendering model. Two axes survive as user-facing knobs; a third apparent axis dissolves into automatic behavior driven by salience composition.  USER AXES: - VISIBILITY = section tiers. Generalizes plan-section-tier-0 (instance #1) from binary visible/hidden to gradation. Tier 0 always renders body; higher tiers may render counts-only or suppress. Replaces Fidelity.visible boolean. - DEPTH = -v / -vv. Currently governs per-item detail (fact body unfurling). Extended: also governs per-section budget. One knob, two effects, both meaning give-me-more.  AUTOMATIC BEHAVIOR (not a third axis): - SALIENCE = composition of derived (kind, key) sets. Joins derived-keys-as-focus-filter as instance #4: refs union window.added union window.updated union stale-keys union cite-count. - TRUNCATION = budget cut respects salience priority. Recency-blind clipping (verbosity-fidelity-review symptoms 2/3) dissolves: when a section exceeds budget, sort by salience, drop tail.  DISSOLUTION RECORD: The four symptoms of verbosity-fidelity-review point at one root: salience exists but truncation is salience-blind. Symptom 1 (kinds counted not rendered) dissolved by tier model. Symptoms 2/3 (fresh items hidden, recency unhonored) dissolve by salience-ranked cut. Symptom 4 (-v/-vv only expands detail) dissolves by depth governing both detail and budget. No new vocabulary needed; existing axes do more work.  CONSEQUENCE FOR LIGHTWEIGHT-EMISSION-ERGONOMICS: Inbound-cite count is a derived (kind, key) set: same shape as inbound-ref count, window deltas, staleness. Plan/lightweight-emission step 2 (left-arrow N cites in landing) is therefore not a separate concern; it is another instance of derived-keys-as-focus-filter feeding the same _compute_marks composition. The two threads were the same work; this decision absorbs both into one frame.  DISSOLUTION-BLIND-SPOT NOTE: Initial framing proposed three orthogonal axes (visibility, depth, truncation). Dissolution test ran late: the third axis collapsed into automatic behavior of the first two. siftd-mining surfaced the prior-session articulation that confirmed the dissolution. Captured as third-occurrence instance.
design/key-prefix-as-fold-key-aware-filter-primitive                high   2  11  2026-05-15  Decision (refined 2026-05-15 after InferioMinion review): expose namespace/prefix filtering via a single kind-aware --key <prefix> flag on loops read. SEMANTICS CONFIRMED: prefix matching, not equality. Implementation is payload.get(fold_key_field).startswith(prefix). User controls specificity by how much of the key they type — '--key dao/' returns the whole subtree; '--key dao/as-url-conventions' returns that single item (prefix-of-itself with nothing longer matching). No --key-exact flag; if you want exact, type the full key. Rationale for prefix-default: namespace drilldown is the dominant use case (operator types the discriminating prefix, gets the subtree); exact-match falls out naturally as the degenerate prefix case. Original dissolution argument: the fold-key field varies by kind (topic for decision/observation; name for thread/task/hypothesis/etc.); the spec already declares which field per kind. --key honors that declaration — one filter operation, kind-aware via existing fold-key spec. Separate flags (--topic/--name/--namespace) would split one operation across N field-name aliases and require enumeration. Evidence sites: (1) fold lens already partitions output by namespace at render — asymmetric to be missing at filter; (2) InferioMinion cross-arc recognition ('oooh' on first sight); (3) InferioMinion second-pass confirmation — independently arrived at name-prefix as simpler dependency structure than separate context field; specifically asked 'does --key do prefix matching or exact matching' confirming the operation is being thought about correctly. Implementation: ~30 LOC in read parser + fetch_fold. Sibling primitive: lens fetch kwargs passthrough (design/lens-fetch-kwargs-passthrough) — both ship together as the access-primitives batch.

Scope: ~600 LOC across 7 files (fetch_trace+walk_refs ~150, lenses/trace.py ~140, _run_trace ~70, tests ~250). One-session work post-orientation. Subtlety to document: under fold-merge, FoldItem.refs is the UNION across upserts — --refs walks lifetime ref set, not per-fact refs (per-fact is v2 if asked). Friction cleanup post-ship: lineage-view-missing resolves directly. Future changelog entries may be partially auto-generated via 'sl trace --since 7d --kind decision'. rendering/visibility-as-gate                                        high   1  11  2026-03-19  Fidelity.visible gates which concern layers render in the fold lens. Depth controls disclosure within each gated layer. Without a visibility flag, the layer is absent regardless of depth. With it, depth dials from badge (MINIMAL) through inline expansion (DETAILED) to full payload (FULL). Three initial layers: refs (structural connections), facts (temporal history), ticks (boundary rhythm). They compose because they are orthogonal dimensions of the same items. Partial dissolution: stream becomes read --facts organized by fold position.
design/cite-as-attention-signal                                     high   1  11  2026-04-24  Citation as attention signal. Syntax: loops cite VERTEX REF1 REF2 ... [--context NAME]. Positional refs become a single comma-separated ref= payload. Kind=cite is a collect-fold declared per vertex (items collect 0 = unbounded). The command is a thin wrapper translating to emit VERTEX cite ref=R1 ref=R2 ... then delegating to _run_emit. Lenses skip cite in display via _SKIP_KINDS but _compute_inbound_refs still iterates it for salience contribution. Vocabulary choice: cite over ping. During design sessions the references aren't presence signals, they're citations — prior work informing current work. 'I cited design/lens-is-the-interface while building session_landing' is semantically accurate; ping isn't. Dissolves into: emit, collect-fold, atoms/refs-on-any-fold, derived-keys-as-focus-filter. Supersedes design/ping-as-attention-signal.
design/peer-grant-extension-not-greenfield                          high   1  11  2026-05-13  Decision (from Explore findings 2026-05-13): engine.Peer/Grant exist in libs/engine/src/engine/peer.py with shape Peer(name, horizon, potential) + Grant(horizon, potential) + grant/restrict/delegate operations + 20 passing tests. horizon=read-constraint, potential=emit-constraint, both frozenset[str] of kinds. This IS the generic substrate version of vouch's scope and sqlmerge's slice — per-vertex specializations live in payload, not in engine. Concrete additions are SMALLER than greenfield framing: (1) add iss to Peer, (2) lift Grant from in-process object to kind=grant Fact with envelope+payload, (3) parent_ref chain semantics, (4) extract receive-gate to VertexPolicy interface, (5) chain_walk + grants_for helpers. The in-process Grant becomes the payload of kind=grant Facts; existing delegate() becomes 'emit Fact with parent_ref'; vertex.receive gate logic moves into VertexPolicy.verify_emission. Solo work unchanged (permissive default policy preserves current behavior). The work is EXTEND not BUILD.
design/sign-on-emit-verify-on-receive                               high   1  11  2026-05-16  Verdict 2026-05-16: signing is constitutive of emit, verification is constitutive of receive — both run by default for vertices with verification policy configured. No separate auth_emit/gated_receive wrapper pair. The signature lives on the Fact atom (Fact.signature, structural per design/attestation-substrate-with-progressive-policy) and is part of the fact's structural identity. Sign uses observer's key (vertex bootstrap generates one at init); verify uses Peer.key from local registry (federated-trust path adds vouch credential lookup per-fact for non-local observers). Verification policy per-vertex (strict/lenient/legacy-accept). Replaces the integration-point framing of design/auth-emit-and-gated-receive-as-wire-identity-translation — there are no separate integration points, just emit and receive doing their constitutive work. OPEN: does engine import vouch directly or does vouch register verifier callback? Affects whether engine has vouch in its dependency graph. Owed in substrate session.

design/lens-declares-fetch                                          high   3   8  2026-04-24  Lens modules may export a fetch callable alongside their view function. When present, the CLI uses the lens-declared fetch instead of the default command fetch. Signature: fetch(vertex_path, **kwargs) -> Any — returned value is the data shape the lens's view function consumes. Pure-lens convention preserved: view function stays (data, zoom, width) -> Block; IO lives in the separate fetch callable. First consumer: session_landing (composes FoldState with tuple[TickWindow, ...]). This is the concrete shape of lens-is-the-interface: lens owns complete I/O contract, not just rendering. Implementation touched: rendering/fold-palette (reused), atoms/n-on-fold-item (item.n for salience), rendering/n-aware-fold-lens (salience-descending sort pattern).
design/loops-as-substrate-not-host                                  high   1  10  2026-05-13  Decision (reframe per Kyle 2026-05-13): loops is the substrate these consumers (sqlmerge, comms, pile, vouch, siftd) are approximating, not a host that accommodates them. The work is completing the substrate so they can stop approximating. Implications: (1) iss is trust-domain BOUNDARY, not Peer metadata — the policy join point where same-iss=intra-domain, cross-iss=federation, unknown-iss=rejected; (2) transport is SUBSTRATE — loops ships the contract (authenticated tick-stream + grant-bound slicing), consumers ship the wire (SSH, HTTP, MCP, etc.); (3) .vertex/KDL is 80%-case convenience, NOT ceiling — extensibility floor stays at Python (VertexPolicy classes, Transport implementations), KDL is one elevation above. Stops migration-shaped thinking; the consumers are loops-shapes at varying fidelity. iss stays opaque-string at data layer; structure goes into VertexPolicy machinery (resolver, trust-assessor, cross-iss chain handling). Peer/Grant were aspirational; this is the concretization.
design/credential-is-grant-in-envelope                              high   4   7  2026-05-16  REFINED 2026-05-16 (fourth position, per-fact-validation correction from advisor + attestation-walk scope-narrowing): credential dissolves to (Identity + wire-Grant) + binding envelope + signature, validated PER-FACT for federated observers (NOT cached after first verification — credential expiration must be checked each time; cached-key-without-expiration would be a security regression). Envelope/signature structural claim intact. vouch.verify returns Identity + wire-Grant — a wire-Peer, not a substrate-Peer. The substrate's Peer for that identity is fetched from vertex-local config using Identity.name as lookup. PRIOR CORRECTIONS preserved: (3rd pass) no AudienceConfig — verifier holds trusted-key config (jwks_urls); Issuer holds signing identity; audience parametric on calls. NEW CORRECTION (this pass): vouch is the federated-trust path INSIDE attestation (per design/three-layer-auth-composition + design/attestation-as-different-ops-sharing-name), NOT 'the attestation layer' itself. Direct-trust observers (local Peer.key registered) bypass vouch entirely — emit signs, receive verifies against Peer.key directly. Vouch loads only when receive encounters an observer not in local Peer registry. Vouch's job: per-fact key-discovery + authority-bridge for federated case.
paradigm/tick-as-weighted-fact                                      high   1   9  2026-03-19  A Tick is not a summary of facts. It is a fact that carries its own density (how many observations compressed) and depth (full fold structure as payload). When it re-enters as input to the next level, that weight is just data — observable, foldable, attendable. Same primitives, one level up. This is why the strange loop works without new mechanisms at each level.
design/fact-signing-enforcement-deferred                            high   1   9  2026-06-13  Kyle ratified 2026-06-13: DEFER the fact-signing require-on-emit gate AND verify-on-receive to the transport/peer era; make DISCLOSURE honest first. Dissolution reasoning: require-on-emit with no verify-on-receive buys only a locally-complete ledger so verify/disclosure can claim all-post-era-keyed-facts-signed — enforcement in service of disclosure, not of a receiver; no untrusted cross-store receive path exists yet, so build the gate when something is on the other side of it. Counter weighed and overridden for facts: the tick-side delta-2 posture (signing is structural from this point forward) would extend down to facts for a clean-from-here ledger that makes eventual verify-on-receive cheap; rejected now because the clean-ledger benefit is disclosure-facing and achievable instead by honest disclosure of the opportunistic reality, and fact-signing is per-observer/opportunistic vs ticks vertex-self-signed at a single funnel. Net: signing stays opportunistic-on-emit + audit-on-demand (store verify); the require/verify layer reactivates when transport/peer gives verify-on-receive a consumer.
paradigm/three-shapes-recursive                                     high   1   8  2026-03-19  The three shapes (observation, accumulation, attention) apply recursively. The data trifecta is not new axes — it is the three shapes applied to attention itself. Observation of attention: n (count of facts at a key). Accumulation of attention: refs (connections between positions). Attention on attention: the system attending to its own attention patterns to determine salience. The renderer trifecta (visibility x depth x density) is the same recursion in display space. The gripping hand in each trifecta is the recursive step.
architecture/vertex-as-complete-contract                            high   2   7  2026-03-25  SUPERSEDED by architecture/loop-as-runtime. The vertex is not the complete I/O contract — the loop is. Sources, fold, boundary, operations attach to loops. Vertex is a named convergence loop with a store.
design/grant-is-structural-primitive-applied-per-layer              high   1   8  2026-05-16  Resolution from 2026-05-15 vocabulary walk (scope↔potential under validator-lambda lens): Grant (horizon + potential) is a structural primitive — a shape that says 'what's visible, what's actionable.' It applies at multiple layers, each with its own vocabulary. Wire-Grant (in credentials): horizon=readable actions, potential=invocable actions; vocabulary is action-shaped (provision-domain, push-facts); issued by vouch, scoped to audience. Substrate-Grant (in engine.peer): horizon=visible kinds, potential=emittable kinds; vocabulary is kind-shaped (domain.provisioned, validator.result); configured per-vertex. SAME STRUCTURE, DIFFERENT VOCABULARY. They do not translate to each other. Linked by identity (observer-name appears in both layers) and nothing else. The dissolution-test for scope↔potential resolved by SEPARATION, not unification — sometimes the dissolution is to recognize sibling applications of a primitive, not to merge them. Caught 2026-05-15 by Kyle pushing the validator-lambda walk past the easy-merge framing.
design/surface-architecture-pared-to-keystone                       high   1   8  2026-06-27  Stress-tested architecture (2026-06-27). Core: a frozen Surface value (flat ordered Rows + per-kind KindView render-hints + a Window provenance record) interposed at the dispatch seam between fetch and render. A Row = a FoldItem plus materialized inbound/salience + an address; built ~1:1 from atoms. All ops (search/filter/select/budget/count/whole) are typed transforms on the Surface BEFORE either encoder runs; render(plain/styled) and to_dict(json) are the last optional step -> json/plain parity. Net-new is SMALL (one painted-free surface.py + the four salience helpers LIFTED from fold.py byte-for-byte); most pains close via dissolution/re-bind. The keystone survives the dissolution test for ONE precise reason: json/plain parity + server-side projection need a structured intermediate that is neither FoldState nor Block; a few flags cannot serve that. STRESS PARED BACK (build ahead of measured need): SHIP keystone + render-only encoders + eq-only predicate + emit grammar fixes + retract; DEFER views{}-as-data authoring framework, neq/prefix operators, Tier-C transform modules, gc/migrate, interactive TUI -- all behind observed demand. Full design: docs/dev/structured-surface-architecture-2026-06-27.md.
design/presentation-register-keys-on-channel                        high   1   8  2026-06-29  Dropping the truncation budget from human reads forced a decouple: width=None now means "no truncation" on BOTH channels, so `width is None` could no longer serve double-duty as the piped-vs-human signal (it had silently conflated truncation-policy with presentation-register). Split them: width:int|None = truncation policy; explicit piped:bool = presentation register (terse `## KIND (N)` for pipes vs friendly `Threads (N):` for humans). fold_view gains a `piped` kwarg; dispatch carries it via render_context={piped: not ctx.isatty} — channel = isatty, the one honest signal. Direct/legacy callers (autoresearch re-export, identity_prompt, goldens) omit it and fall to the old width-is-None proxy (back-compat, zero golden drift). Sole Operation render site is fold.py:543 (emit is render_lens=None) so no sibling path misses the flag. Shipped c4db11f, 1504 green + 3-case guard. The conflation was the bug; the fix is one explicit flag replacing an overloaded proxy (explicit-over-implicit).

paradigm/boundaries-as-driven-conditions                            high   1   7  2026-04-28  STRANGE-LOOPS line 7 declares 'Time is fundamental'; line 106 invokes 'timer ticks' as a constituent observation in the auth-failure example. The conceptual model has time-as-trigger; the engine doesn't. RSS-feed-reader lineage produced an implementation where every boundary type is content-triggered (count, kind/match, predicate — all fired by fact arrival via vertex.receive). Reframe: a boundary is a period-completion CONDITION on signs flowing through a CHANNEL. Each channel has a DRIVER that produces sign-events. Channels include — fact-stream (driver: receive), fold-state (driver: receive re-evaluation), clock (driver: tick scheduler), peer-signal (driver: notify/wake), sibling-tick (driver: cascade), observer (driver: manual fire). 'Driver' is working vocabulary — chosen for flexibility because clock/time would have implied linear-monotonic-externally-imposed and excluded manual-fire, notify, sibling-tick. The unifying axis is 'what fires the period close' regardless of source. Implications — (1) emit-skips-boundary-catchup dissolves UP not sideways: emit handles content live, driver-fired boundaries fire from their own drivers, evaluate_boundaries collapses to one-shot post-replay reconciliation inside load_vertex_program. (2) Engine boundary types expand: boundary_elapsed/at/idle as siblings of existing types. (3) notify-as-vertex-capability and manual-tick-emission are the same primitive at different positions — both are non-receive drivers. (4) Today's dispatch-consolidation-via-program survives unchanged: program._dispatch_tick is universal across all drivers — accidentally built the right shape for the future. Audit prerequisite: walk _fire_live_boundaries to confirm live-fire completeness before claiming the dissolution holds. Larger umwelt reframe parked separately as thread/umwelt-as-paradigm-frame.
engine/peer-grant-separation-validated-by-vouch                     high   1   7  2026-05-13  Decision (2026-05-13): the Jan 27-30 dissolution that split bundled Peer into Observer-on-Fact + Grant-at-Vertex + convenience-Peer is validated as right-shaped by vouch — first real consumer of engine.Peer/Grant. Evidence from explore/peer-grant subtask (~/Code/vouch commit d95d36a, friction doc Obs 5): vouch needs grant_of(peer) for cross-vouch scope comparison; Grant is exactly the policy half stripped of identity that vouch's payload needs (frozen, hashable, set-shaped, value-equal); Peer/Grant separation matches ADR-0001's stance that scope is per-vouch not per-agent. Implication: any future engine recast that proposes re-fusing Peer and Grant must justify against this consumer's validated benefit. This is the loops-side positive anchor — architectural bet paid off, recorded so future-me (or whoever's tempted to re-fuse) reads the validation before tempting backsliding.
design/vouch-rescission-fact-level-not-lattice                      high   1   7  2026-05-13  Verdict: vouch rescission is Fact-level, not a lattice operation. Substrate stays monotone. Evidence: libs/engine/src/engine/peer.py is monotone by construction — restrict_grant intersects, expand_grant only widens within parent bounds, delegate narrows. Grant.minus() would be the first non-monotone op and break the issuance-chain invariant. Framing: same shape as write-receipt-vs-temporal-query (#agent-party 04-29) and fold-view-vs-fact-history (alcove convergence 05-10). Issuance and rescission are writes (Facts); active scope at time t is a fold-derived temporal query, racy with next writer by definition. ADR-0001 already commits to temporal derivation via TTL — rescission is event-driven generalization of TTL decay. Discriminating question (substrate-overreach filter): no second consumer for Grant.minus today at issuance path — rescission targets prior issuance, doesn't carve future one. Verification is replay, not lattice op. N=1, not N=2. Operational discipline: 'treat rescission as event-stream fold, not Grant ∖ Grant' lands as a VouchPolicy discipline (the substrate-doesn't-enforce list), alongside scrivener's earlier four. Tradeoff honestly: verifiers can't validate JWT in isolation, need replay over rescission stream — but TTL imposes the same cost (need a clock), so substrate pays nothing new. Surfaced 2026-05-13 #vouch-impl by scrivener post-issue_vouch-e2e; reply at message 1600.

paradigm/peer-attention-loop                                        high   1   6  2026-03-19  When multiple observers share a fold, the strange loop runs through participants. My attention patterns become observable facts in your context, shaping your attention, producing observations that shape mine. The collective attention is visible to all observers through the same fold state. This is why n on FoldItem matters for peers — it measures collective observation density, not individual.

design/lens-as-navigation-vs-lens-as-answer                         high   1   6  2026-05-15  Decision (refinement of design/lens-is-the-interface): lenses split into two shapes by job — navigation lenses (route attention to drilldowns) vs content lenses (deliver the answer directly). Both are valid; conflating them produces lenses that do both badly. Origin: InferioMinion 2026-05-15 articulated for guidance lens — 'the lens's job is namespace discovery, not content delivery. It answers what namespaces have guidance, not what each guide says. Content lives in the patterns the guides route to.' Generalizes beyond guidance. Navigation lens design constraints: (1) surface namespace-level (not just per-item) salience as the discrimination signal — operator needs to know WHERE to drill next, not just that drillable things exist; (2) prefer counts + ref-graph aggregates over body content in the index render; (3) make the drilldown command obvious (e.g. 'patterns: dao/ 47 items ←128' implies 'loops read X --kind pattern --key dao/'). Content lens design constraints: (1) front-load verdict in first ~140 chars (preview budget for first-disclosure); (2) HYPOTHESIS-shaped bodies (verdict + evidence + conclusion) so drill-down decisions are earned not triggered; (3) progressive disclosure across zoom levels. Examples by shape: navigation lenses — guidance (proposed), session_landing (core loops), reconcile (partial — routes attention to stale items but also delivers their status); content lenses — fold (default), painted record line, search results, decision body at -v. Implications: (a) lens authors should declare which shape they're building; (b) painted utilities may eventually split into navigation-render helpers vs content-render helpers; (c) the lens-as-router pattern is the natural home for --key drilldown — the navigation lens routes you to the prefix, --key delivers the slice.
design/transport-boundary-is-bytes-not-facts                        high   1   6  2026-05-16  Finding from reading libs/store/transport.py: Transport does not understand facts, ticks, or vertices — it moves SQLite files. Protocol-based with push(local_path, remote_path)/pull(remote_path, local_path). Current impl LocalTransport (file copy). SSH flagged future. HTTP not yet implemented. Implication for vouch integration: wire-auth gates the slice-push, not per-fact-emission. Vouch JWT gates 'principal P can push to endpoint'; semantic filtering (which kinds, which observers) is downstream via Peer/Grant on receive. The byte-boundary makes the three-layer auth composition possible.

(1) --refs [N] unifies fetch-walk + render-decoration: bare --refs walks depth 1 and decorates edges (← inbound, → outbound) per item; --refs N walks N hops; omitted = no walk no decoration. Drops the prior render-side filter behavior — orphan items render with (no refs) marker rather than disappearing. (2) Positional kind/key on read: sl read project decision/design/foo parses as --kind decision --key design/foo. --kind/--key flags retained as backstop. (3) --diff lands on read: cumulative field-deltas rendering (status: old → new, refs: +added -removed per emit) moves from trace lens into read dispatch. Solves the single unique capability trace had beyond read. (4) Render shape is graph-decorated, not chronologically-interleaved (trace was). Anchored entity renders with full body + edge list underneath; ref-walked entities render below the anchor with ┄ via ← kind/key ┄ markers identifying how each came in; depth-2+ nests under depth-1 parents with ↳ prefix + indent; cycles back to already-rendered items dim rather than re-render. Dissolution: no rename of old read --refs (visibility toggle) needed — unified --refs semantic supersedes it. Trace command deleted, not deprecated (no external ship). design/tick-signing-era-is-a-floor                                  high   1   6  2026-06-14  Kyle ratified 2026-06-14 (Gate-B floor): once a store starts signing at the TICK level, it must continue — the era-regression guard (no unsigned tick after a signed tick) is a non-negotiable FLOOR, not a per-vertex flag. Rationale: era-monotonicity is witness-chain INTEGRITY, not vertex POLICY — verify already condemns the regressed state (CHAIN BROKEN) and reanchor already refuses to create it; seal must match (closes the say/do gap where seal could mint exactly what verify forbids). Friction is low in the SSH sense: the private key is local, so signing is transparent/automatic while present; the cost only appears when the key is ABSENT, and then the right behavior is SSH's — a hard STOP, never a silent downgrade to unauthenticated. So seal REFUSES (not warn-and-proceed) to mint an unsigned tick in the signed era. Degrades gracefully: emit stays opportunistic so the window's FACTS are still stored; only the attestation boundary (tick) is withheld, and the next successful seal closes the accumulated window — data preserved, attestation deferred, never falsified. Disclosure is the floor under all of it: every signing action states signed/unsigned + reason regardless of the refuse/proceed branch. Distinct from the still-deferred FACT-signing require gate (decision:design/fact-signing-enforcement-deferred): facts stay opportunistic (mixed signed/unsigned is normal, live edge strippable); only TICKS take the structural floor, matching the delta-2 "signing is structural from this point forward" posture. The forward-policy "require signing" vertex flag (Gate A) remains a SEPARATE, optional, default-off knob — it governs whether a vertex must sign AT ALL (the first signature, optionally facts), not whether it may stop. Open forward work: the transport era breaks the "key is always local" assumption — see thread:transport-era-signing-key-flow.

design/salience-max-propagation                                     high   1   6  2026-07-02  RATIFIED (Kyle 2026-07-02): salience for non-fact nodes = defined ONCE at KEY level (three-term contract as ratified — inbound-refs target kind:key, coverage is an identity property, only recency is fact-native); FACTS INHERIT their key's salience (stream rail shows the fold-salience of the identity each event touched — same number, other axis); CONTAINERS (kind, vertex, tick) AGGREGATE BY MAX, not sum — the rail is a scent trail ('is there anything hot in here'), mass is already shown explicitly (counts/share/⊃). design/dispatch-consolidation-via-program                           high   1   5  2026-04-28  Run-clause dispatch consolidates from 3 CLI sites (emit.py:344, sync.py:105 combine-child, sync.py:259 main) into VertexProgram. Shape: load_vertex_program(path, *, run_dispatcher=callable) injects a (command, tick_name, vertex_path) -> None callback; program.receive(fact) wraps vertex.receive and dispatches if tick.run; program.sync internalizes the dispatch loop over result.ticks. Engine stays subprocess-free via injection — engine knows THAT a callback fires, not what shell execution looks like. Concurrent cleanup: program.vertex.X reaches in CLI and tests (~9 sites) move to program.receive / program.name / program.has_store. _execute_boundary_run stays in apps/loops, hlab inlines its own copy until a third consumer forces extraction. Replay safety verified: vertex.receive short-circuits on _replaying flag (vertex.py:433), and replay path bypasses receive entirely (calls fold_one_mut/loop.receive directly). Behavior change to acknowledge: emit.py:329 seed-fact loop and emit.py:567 session-close path will start firing run-clauses they currently silently drop — both ARE the fragility being fixed. Asymmetry surfaced separately as thread emit-skips-boundary-catchup.

architecture/id-primitive-python-ulid                               high   1   5  2026-05-17  DECISION 2026-05-16: SqliteStore id generation uses python-ulid (str(ULID())) — pure-Python, no C extension, time-sortable, 26-char Crockford base32. CHOSEN OVER (a) uuid.uuid7() stdlib — would match the post-regression uuid4 string shape and visually blend the wedge into the future; we explicitly DON'T want that (the wedge is a discrete bug-class era and should remain visible); (b) sqlite-ulid C extension — answers a question we no longer ask (SQL-side id generation via DEFAULT). When the regression moved id gen from SQL-side DEFAULT (ulid()) to Python-side _gen_id() it ALSO removed the architectural need for a SQL-callable ulid() function; the extension's only remaining advantage is per-id gen cost (0.35μs vs 2.3μs) which is dominated by file I/O on emit anyway. PROPERTIES re-derived from use case: (1) globally unique across machines/processes/peers — required for cross-store merge dedup via INSERT OR IGNORE on PK; (2) time-sortable lexicographically — required for chronological fact interleaving across stores and for ORDER BY id semantics; (3) cheap to generate — emit path opens/closes connection per invocation, but the dominant cost is SQLite open not id gen; (4) content-addressing NOT required — same fact emitted to two stores legitimately gets two different ids (merge dedup is per-fact identity, not per-content); (5) replayable — store is durable, ids must survive forever. python-ulid satisfies (1)-(5) cleanly. WITHIN-MS MONOTONICITY CAVEAT: python-ulid's default ULID() constructor generates fresh random suffix per call — NOT monotonic within a millisecond. Fine for uniqueness and dedup; means ORDER BY id within the same ms is random across calls in the same process. If we ever need within-ms monotonicity, python-ulid offers monotonic helpers; not needed today. CONTINUITY: matches the pre-Mar-15 id format already in existing stores, so post-fix ids visually continuous with the original ULID era; the 2026-03-15 to fix-date uuid4 wedge stands out as discrete. RATIONALE-FOR-RATIONALE: this decision exists in part because the 2026-03-15 regression happened WITHOUT a decision of record naming why ULID was chosen — only a comment in code citing 'merge compatibility with libs/store' which the perf optimization read past. Naming the substrate properties as a decision means the next optimizer reads the rationale before swapping the implementation.

paradigm/agent-as-compiler-not-operator                             high   1   5  2026-05-20  Agent compiles an immutable execution manifest; human signs the manifest; infrastructure executes — agent is courier, never operator. The signed thing IS the compiled intent, not a capability grant. Reframes vouch flow: discovery (low-risk broad read) → compile (agent produces deterministic payload) → attestation (peer signs exact payload) → execution (infra replays signed payload). Surfaced via Gemini exchange 2026-05-20; Kyle pulled it out as the load-bearing reframe. Maps onto sign-on-emit/verify-on-receive: the 'execution manifest' IS a Fact with specific kind; signature IS the attestation; execution boundary triggers on attested-fact existence in scope. Reframes multi-endpoint problem — target service doesn't expose N privileged endpoints to untrusted agents; it exposes a single 'execute-attested-fact' boundary that reads payload from the signed fact body. This is the loops-paradigm answer to the enterprise-IAM Registry pattern: facts → boundary → execution, with attestation as the gate. Industry drafts (Prakash/AIP) building inline runtime proxies with regex filters get dissolved by this framing — once the agent is a compiler not an operator, there's nothing on the wire to babysit. The threat surface compresses to (a) discovery-phase read exfiltration, still open, and (b) compile-time argument injection between human-review and infrastructure-execution, closed by signature-binds-exact-payload.
design/tick-signature-on-every-tick                                 high   1   5  2026-06-09  Delta 2 shape: signature column on EVERY tick row, computed in append_tick over the existing _tick_row_hash (which commits to prev_hash + window_hash, so each signature transitively covers everything behind it). No head-anchor artifact — a separate head record is a mutable pointer wearing an anchor costume (write-receipt principle); the tick IS the commitment shape, the signature belongs on the commitment. Dissolves 'the head' as a special case: every tick self-verifying, head is just the newest. Pre-signature ticks render as era, never retro-claimed — same move as delta 1's chain columns. Cost negligible at session-boundary cadence. Also the rehearsal for delta 3 (Fact.signature): same pattern one layer up, proven first where rows number ~200 not ~2000. Kyle's framing sharpened it: the decision is 'signing is structural from this point forward', not 'patch the head'. External witnessing (publish head hash outside the store) noted as a complement, not an alternative — not this delta.

design/horizon-unarmed-rollup                                       high   2   4  2026-07-06  AMENDED (Kyle 2026-07-05, build-review ruling): unarmed = uncovered by ANY declared trigger, not merely 'no own boundary'. Observer-asymmetry is necessary but not sufficient for authority. Counter-examples: chord+loops-claude (symmetric co-formation, each sees different things, no authority); Herald+relay (domain-asymmetric, different views, no authority). Refined: meaningful authority requires observer-asymmetry as precondition, but observer-asymmetry without lever-of-action is peer-relationship-across-perspectives, not authority. Final taxonomy: domain-asymmetric, symmetric co-formation, steward-asymmetric (absorbs old 'authority-asymmetric'). Observer-asymmetry is present in all three but only becomes stewardship when paired with an operational lever. Three shapes, not four — but for the right reason.

design/antipode-five-readings                                       mid    2   3  2026-05-09  The antipode operation has five distinct readings: (A) antipode lands on explicit rejection decision in corpus — dichotomy was real and resolved; (B) convergent antipodes across clusters point to shared rejection — implicit cross-cutting principle the project applies but never names; (C) antipode genuinely distant with no near match — direction unexplored or principle robustly anti the antipode-direction; (D) synthesis failure — antipode embedding within ~0.06 of cluster centroid means LLM produced re-description not inversion; (E) antipode lands in adjacent cluster — coexisting mechanisms, not opposites. practice/multi-prefix-emit-as-routing-paths                         mid    2   3  2026-05-15  Practice (refined 2026-05-15 after InferioMinion's divergent-probes extension): when a conceptual entity has multiple natural namespace homes, emit it under each — two facts with different prefixes, same body — rather than introducing a separate 'context' or 'tag' field. The duplicate emits ARE the multi-routing semantics. SHARPENED FRAMING (InferioMinion): two emits aren't just routing aliases, they're INDEPENDENT PROBES measuring which clusters of work actually reference that knowledge. If test/resolver-chain accumulates high salience and settings/resolver-chain stays low, that's evidence the pattern is primarily a testing concern even though it lives in the settings package. The salience signal is RICHER than you'd get from a single canonical entry point — divergence is information, not maintenance burden. Origin: InferioMinion's resolution of the multi-context guides edge case during --key design. Example: a guide for 'when writing tests that touch the settings resolver' belongs to both test/ and settings/. Naive instinct says 'add a multi-value context field.' Dissolution: emit twice as name=test/foo and name=settings/foo — the guide surfaces from either entry point during --key drilldown. Each fold item accumulates independent revision counts, ref graphs, and salience scores. Divergence is signal: each routing path measures a real audience independently. Safety valve (Kyle's framing): if the two paths drift to contradiction, that's loops surfacing a genuine conceptual split — not maintenance problem, but DISCOVERY mechanism. Pattern: fold-key as routing handle; duplicate emits as multiple routes to same content AND as independent measurement probes on the underlying clusters. Generalizes beyond guides: any fact kind where fold-key acts as navigation handle (decision topics, thread names, task names). Discriminator: is the entity conceptually one thing accessed via multiple paths AND served by multiple distinct audience clusters (yes — emit twice, let salience diverge) vs two related things sharing a body (no — emit once, ref between them). Dissolves the recurring temptation to add 'tags' or 'multi-value context' fields to handle multi-classification.
design/scope-and-potential-distinguished-by-layer                   mid    2   3  2026-05-16  REFINED 2026-05-15 (pass-through correction): scope (vouch) and potential (engine.peer) are DISTINGUISHED, not merged. Different layers, different vocabularies, no derivation. Scope is wire-Grant's vocabulary (action-shaped, audience-specific, issued by vouch); potential is substrate-Grant's vocabulary (kind-shaped, vertex-local, set by operator config). Share Grant structural primitive (horizon + potential) but apply different vocabularies — wire-scope to action-vocab, substrate-potential to kind-vocab. Linked by observer-name across layers. design/audience-config-dissolves                                    mid    1   4  2026-05-16  Dissolution finding 2026-05-15 (Kyle caught in pass-through): AudienceConfig dissolves entirely. Carried forward as vestigial after scope/potential walk, where its unpacker field dissolved (no scope-to-potential translation needed). Examining what remained: (1) audience name is a parameter to verify(), not config — caller specifies expected_audience; verify checks JWT.aud matches; (2) key source is verifier-wide or per-issuer (via JWKS discovery), not per-audience — the verifier trusts certain issuers regardless of audience; (3) scope vocabulary is documentation, not runtime data. None of these are per-audience runtime config. Corrected lib surface: Verifier holds trusted-key config (jwks_urls), exposes verify(jwt, expected_audience); Issuer holds signing key and issuer_id, exposes issue(subject, audience, scope, act). Two configs about WHO (trusted issuers, signing identity), not about WHICH AUDIENCE. Audience parametric on calls. Failure mode named: when a walk resolves something by emptying it, the next reading can mistake the emptied container for a residual — the pass-through is the corrective.

design/chain-witness-order                                          mid    1   4  2026-06-09  Chain ordering authority is witness order (rowid), never id order. Window cursors stay fact ids (portable handles); membership and hashing resolve cursor->rowid and walk append order. append_tick cursor = id of newest fact BY ROWID, not MAX(id). Fixes mixed-id-era vacuous windows (uuid4 era sorts above all ULIDs, pinning MAX(id) mid-history forever) AND late-arrival false alarms (backfilled fact with honest old event-ts landed inside a sealed id-window = tamper alarm caused by truthfulness; in witness order it lands on live edge, sealed by next tick as received-now). Deliberate semantics flip pinned in tests: backdated-id arrival is no longer a break; displacing a covered row's rowid is. ULID keeps its job — event order for the read path. Already-minted epoch tick still verifies (empty window hashes identically under both orderings). Known interim consequence on mixed stores: project epoch cursor resolves to rowid 1121/2019, so the NEXT tick seals ~900 pre-epoch facts as-of-seal-time — strictly more protection but coverage does not distinguish sealed-since-receipt from sealed-late; rebirth-with-receipt supersedes.
design/seal-verb                                                    mid    1   4  2026-06-09  sl seal <vertex> -m reason: the deliberately drawn attestation boundary. Dissolves into existing machinery — emit kind=seal + vertex-declared boundary when=seal; no engine or lang changes. The observer driver from boundaries-as-driven-conditions rides the fact-stream: volition enters as a fact. The reason fact is the LAST fact inside the window it seals (attestation covers its own justification; fact_cursor == reason fact id, verified live on tick 3). Must-fire semantics: seal refuses when the writable vertex declares no seal boundary; declared match props fold into the payload. Session close DISSOLVES INTO seal (Kyle's call): project.vertex boundary is now when=seal, SessionEnd hook emits session bookkeeping fact then sl seal — session close is an instance of the general act, not the special case. Use cases unlocked: post-backfill attestation, pre-surgery checkpoint, chord-carving, peer attestation point (store-side analog of vouch transaction endorsement — bind at the boundary). Rebirth/replay-to-store composes as: transform-replay + old-ticks-as-facts + receipt-fact + seal.
design/fact-signing-per-observer-keys                               mid    1   4  2026-06-12  Fact signatures are per-observer authorship claims, Kyle ratified 2026-06-12. Observers without keys emit unsigned — honest NULL becomes a PER-OBSERVER era, generalizing delta 2's per-store epoch. Layering note: this composes with shipped tick signing rather than replacing it — unsigned-author facts still sit under the vertex-key-signed window hash (custody claim); signed-author facts carry both claims. Custody honesty: on a single machine any local process can read any key in .loops/keys/, so observer separation is organizational not adversarial until keys live with their principals (transport/peer era). Companion mechanism: _fact_row_hash goes era-aware (includes signature only when non-NULL) so signature-stripping breaks the sealed window — delta-2 envelope trick, no re-anchoring of pre-signature rows.

paradigm/surfaced-invariant                                         mid    2   2  2026-04-27  Lens (#observations msg 319, 2026-04-27) sharpened the third-leg framing with reproduction property: 'Spec reproduces by being read. Test reproduces by being run. Surfaced-invariant reproduces by being active in the context where the decisions are happening — not lag, not batch, but concurrent.' That's the distinctive property — concurrency with the decision, not before (spec) or after (test). Tonight's session demonstrated it twice in real time: (1) paradigm/design-requires-substrate-first was emitted as a fact, then within minutes was being used by lens to interpret events still happening (msg 314 explicitly cited substrate-recognition as the resolution). (2) The fold-lens wire shipped at msg 301, then the wire itself became substrate for the visible-tag empirical test (msg 309) and the daemon-tool-call shape resolution (DM 306). Principles emitted as facts and continuously surfaced into operator context don't wait for the next session to be read back — they're active during the decisions they constrain. That concurrent-active property is what differentiates surfaced-invariant from spec-doc and test-fixture as design discipline. Implication: for a principle to function as a surfaced-invariant, it must be (a) emitted as a fact in a fold that's continuously visible, (b) read into context at every relevant decision point, (c) phrased so it can be applied at decision time without translation. The flag-guidance-prevents-mis-reach instance (relay msg 316) is what happens when a principle is in the right shape but in the wrong location: the spec was written but didn't reach the call site.
architecture/visible-tag-inclusion-property                         mid    3   1  2026-04-27  Lens (#observations msg 315, 2026-04-27) sharpened the framing: the 'visible' field in Fidelity was designed as inclusion-only by construction, not by convention. The dual-duty in fold.py isn't a deviation from UX intuition — it's a deviation from the designed contract that happened to feel natural because the user wrote both behaviors in one flag. Reframes Relay's earlier UX-cleanliness tension (msg 310): not 'structural cleanliness at UX cost,' but 'restoring the designed contract reveals two UX intentions were accidentally fused.' Unfusing them is MORE honest UX, not less — user gets 'show edge expansion' AND 'filter to connected-only' as separate controls. Decision now has three components: (a) separate inclusion from filtering in Fidelity contract — visible carries inclusion only, filtering moves to a new axis (--filter-X flags or Fidelity.filter); (b) migration path for the one current consumer (--refs/--facts in fold.py); (c) painted-side test catching dual-duty visible use going forward. Lens flagged that (c) is what painted can mechanically enforce; (a) and (b) are cross-library decisions for Kyle/painted-side authority. Empirical evidence (msg 309): both production tags currently violate the contract — convention-not-surviving-scale already breached at scale=2 because dual-duty was the implementation choice from the start.
paradigm/design-requires-substrate-first                            mid    1   3  2026-04-27  Relay (DM 307, 2026-04-27): design coherence sometimes requires substrate to land first. If you commit to a design before the substrate is real, you'll commit to the wrong one — not from bad reasoning but because the cost surface you're optimizing against is hypothetical. Two instances in tonight's session: (1) verbosity redesign needed Fidelity fields to exist as substrate before its vocabulary could land (chars/lines were sitting in painted unwired; once someone pulled them into use, the design language caught up). (2) daemon tool-call emission shape: raw + read-time-filter looked wrong while fold lens couldn't actually filter; once the Fidelity wire shipped (msg 301), the right answer became visible and the original aggregated-at-emit recommendation flipped (DM 306). Both: substrate landed → cost surface changed → design changed. Connects to vocabulary-as-architecture (msg 287-288): vocabulary lags substrate, design lags vocabulary, all three stabilize together. Implication for sequencing: do not pre-commit design when substrate is hypothetical. Do build substrate even when the design isn't named yet — the right design will become visible when the cost surface becomes real. Loops's infrastructure-ahead-of-vocabulary read on Fidelity is an instance of this: building the substrate before the consumers are ready to use it produces the design surface where the right answer can be seen.
paradigm/boundary-as-watcher-triple                                 mid    1   3  2026-04-28  Gripping-hand dissolution of boundary categorization. Prior decision (paradigm/boundaries-as-driven-conditions) split boundaries into content-driven vs driver-fired. The 2026-04-27 live-fire trace surfaced a potential fourth category (state-crossing — fire when fold predicate becomes true regardless of triggering kind). Categorical proliferation is the dissolution-symptom: the categories all instantiate one primitive. A boundary is the triple (watched-state, driver, fire-condition). Today's instances and proposed extensions all collapse — count: (fact-arrival count, receive, count crosses N); kind/match: (fact stream, receive, matching fact arrives); predicate: (fold state, receive on triggering kind, condition true); proposed clock: (wall clock, tick scheduler, elapsed crosses T); proposed notify: (external signal, wake driver, signal arrived); proposed state-crossing: (fold state, fold-mutation driver, condition true). Predicate and state-crossing share an identical fire-condition but use different drivers — same condition, different watcher. Boundary-as-type collapses. New boundary capabilities = new drivers + new watched-states, not new types. Implementation consequences — (1) Duplication between _fire_live_boundaries (vertex.py:440-504) and evaluate_boundaries (vertex.py:696-802) dissolves into a single _check_and_fire_for_fact helper. (2) evaluate_boundaries' real job is replay-suppression catchup — moves to one-shot inside load_vertex_program after vertex.replay(). (3) Sync attenuates dramatically: catchup leaves to post-replay, dispatch is per-program (design/dispatch-consolidation-via-program), only 'run cadenced sources' remains — and that itself is the cadence driver firing, which dissolves further if a daemon hosts drivers continuously. (4) Live-fire is ALREADY complete for every boundary type that exists today — the 'audit live-fire completeness' step from the prior resolution path was a no-op. State-crossing is the only genuinely new shape that requires evaluation-on-every-state-change. The reframe survives the prior one: paradigm/boundaries-as-driven-conditions was the stepping stone; this is its further dissolution. The driver vocabulary survives unchanged. The category vocabulary dissolves.
design/architecture-via-vocabulary                                  mid    2   2  2026-05-09  Instruction-tuned embedders are the right substrate for the structure-reveal lens. The instruction is a real parameter — same content, different user-specified axis, structurally different topology. Robust clusters (Jaccard high across instruction-sweep) reveal the project's crystallized vocabulary; instruction-specific clusters reveal perspective-dependent organizations. Validated empirically on 296 project decisions with E5-Mistral: orientation cluster + search/FTS cluster survive both 'mechanism' and 'domain' instructions (Jaccard 0.78, 0.67); other clusters reshuffle structurally (Jaccard 0.0–0.25). Implication for lens design: instruction is first-class parameter; multi-instruction intersection mode produces a fundamentally different output (the corpus's crystallized vocabulary, bottom-up).

design/wire-not-library-at-trust-boundary-only                      mid    1   3  2026-05-13  Decision: The wire-not-library rule applies at cross-org / cross-language trust boundaries; it does NOT apply to intra-homelab Python services. Evidence: vouch builds on atoms/engine/store directly while still exposing language-agnostic JSON wire envelopes to Go/Rust consumers. The two axes are orthogonal — conflating them implies unnecessary reimplementation of the substrate by every Python service. Origin: I posted the wire-not-library framing to #trust-substrate (msg 1518) without this disambiguation, conflating cross-boundary protocol commitment with cross-repo implementation sharing. Implication: foundational ADR must be explicit so a future reader doesn't conclude wire-not-library means reimplement atoms in vouch. Cross-language consumers see the JSON envelope; Python consumers import the libs that produce it.
design/loops-as-protocol-not-framework                              mid    1   3  2026-05-13  Decision (recovered from #trust-substrate work 01KRGXR58W67, May 12-13): loops is a PROTOCOL with a canonical Python implementation, not a framework. Vouch, comms, pile are applications of the protocol, not applications built with loops. Sharper layer than substrate-not-host (same direction, deeper claim). Implications: (1) Substrate decisions (Peer.iss, VertexPolicy, chain-walk, programmatic construction) are PROTOCOL-LEVEL commitments — propagate to every implementation. (2) libs/sign is IMPLEMENTATION-LEVEL — gruel-network's Python crypto choices, not part of protocol; peer homelabs could implement differently. (3) Applications (vouch) are local to one service. Three-tier evolution: protocol slow + deliberate, implementation local-per-language, application local-per-service. The #trust-substrate room independently derived the same primitive set (observer/timestamp/payload + scope-lattice + event-sourced projections) WITHOUT loops in the room — strongest external validation: alcove + claude-commission recognized loops Fact/Tick/Cascade as the same protocol they were deriving from first principles.

design/vouch-catalog-completeness-fact-payload-cleavage             mid    1   3  2026-05-13  Verdict: vouch emission catalog should enumerate ALL payload keys; jti belongs in catalog (resolves scrivener's d379f76 catalog cross-check). The structural-vs-semantic cleavage IS real in loops — but it lives at the Fact/payload boundary (kind/ts/payload/observer/origin are substrate-universal Fact fields), not within payload. Payload is by construction the domain side; the fold operates on it, lenses interpret it, there is no infrastructure-in-payload-but-not-really-payload tier in loops. Introducing one in vouch's catalog would create a substrate-shape distinction asymmetric with the rest of loops — cleavage-of-convenience. Substrate-overreach test on the alternative ('move jti to Fact-level'): N=1, only vouch has JWT-Fact correlation ids, this is the substrate-feels-universal trap. Refs already handle cross-Fact correlation: future rescission Facts can ref the vouch via ref=vouch:<jti> with jti as fold key. Adjacent: ADR-0002's emission catalog is vouch's instance of the kinds-i-produce registry shape (alcove's 05-10 framing). 'catalog-or-it-doesn't-count' discipline is structurally the same shape as 'drift-detector asks what kinds emit that I'm not measuring.' Scrivener's payload_shape-keys-==-emitted-payload-keys check is the cross-validation step that shape needs. Surfaced 2026-05-13 #vouch-impl post-exercise-2; reply at message 1602.
paradigm/capability-projecting-vs-identity-asserting-writes         mid    1   3  2026-05-13  Substrate framing surfaced 2026-05-13 #vouch-impl during rescission write-path design (scrivener msg 1613). Verdict: write operations partition by what their authorization is checking. Capability-projecting writes bind new capability into a chain; auth is forward-looking (does actor currently have authority?); requires checking current state. Identity-asserting writes assert pre-existing relation in chain; auth is backward-looking (was actor the one who established the relation?); requires checking historical state. Issuance is canonical capability-projecting (resolve_voucher projects current group-membership to capability). Rescission is canonical identity-asserting ('I was the voucher of V' is a fact about Fact-ancestry). Coupling rescission auth to current capability would mean a Fellow whose anchor was revoked loses ability to rescind their own prior vouches — their issuances become irrevocable in their absence, worst failure mode for a system that exists to enable revocation. Generalization: any system distinguishing 'grant' from 'revoke-my-grant' has this shape (permission systems, trust networks, claim issuance/withdrawal, attestation/recantation). Principle: if the operation asserts a historical relation, identity-anchor it; if it projects new capability, capability-anchor it. Operational discriminator at design time: 'does this write require knowing current state of X to authorize, or knowing past state of X?' That question partitions the operation. Adjacent to write-receipt-vs-temporal-query (same temporal axis applied to auth shape rather than return shape). Reply at message 1614.
pattern/runtime-model-assumption-leak                               mid    1   3  2026-05-14  Substrate framing surfaced 2026-05-13 #vouch-impl during service-shell exercise; landed durable on vouch main 7958fe5 in docs/friction/service-shell-exercise.md Obs 2. (Re-emit as decision; earlier observation-kind emit was orphaned because project vertex doesn't declare observation kind.) loops substrate was shaped under single-threaded CLI assumptions; vouch (first concurrent-runtime consumer) surfaced the first instance: SqliteStore connection is thread-affine, sqlite3.connect() without check_same_thread=False at libs/engine/src/engine/sqlite_store.py:99. Consumer-owns-threading is the right resolution at N=1 — same shape as VouchPolicy substrate-doesn't-enforce disciplines. Three substrate options rejected/accepted: (a) check_same_thread=False NOT safe relax (WAL corruption without consumer-side locking); (b) connection-per-thread pool is substrate change for N=1 AND pool shape is consumer-runtime-dependent (Litestar workers vs trio nursery vs asyncio task group); (c) consumer-owns-threading correct. At N=2 the substrate-side action is documentation (SqliteStore docstring), not implementation change. Latent assumption-leak candidates for eventual review: does emit block on fsync? is there a streaming-write contract? does replay assume monotonic ts under concurrent writes? Meta-pattern: 'first concurrent consumer surfaces substrate assumptions' — future instances should be obvious-shape because we've named it.
design/lens-fetch-kwargs-passthrough                                mid    1   3  2026-05-15  Decision: complete the lens-declares-fetch contract by threading arbitrary --flag=value CLI args through to the lens's fetch() kwargs, symmetric to how call_lens already passes optional kwargs to render functions (lens_resolver.py:229-233). Current state: main.py:597-600 passes a fixed set (kind, observer, retain_facts) to lens_fetch — lenses CAN declare def fetch(vertex_path, **kwargs) but the CLI has nothing to put in the kwargs bag beyond those three. Result: lens-declares-fetch is half-wired — lenses can declare custom fetch but cannot be parameterized at the CLI surface. Evidence: InferioMinion's guidance lens hardcodes 'Access:' instructions including 'loops read X --filter pattern' — a flag that doesn't exist. The lens is documenting an aspirational CLI surface, indicating the gap is felt at their site. Their guide kind groups by payload.context (not key namespace), so --key alone can't drill into 'When Working on Authorization' sections; the lens needs to declare its own --context filter and have it threaded through. Implementation: parse unknown --foo=bar / --foo bar args in the read parser into a dict, pass as **lens_kwargs alongside the standard kwargs. ~20 line change in main.py. Lenses opt in by declaring **kwargs in their fetch signature; existing lenses unaffected. Sibling to --key (decision/key-prefix-as-fold-key-aware-filter-primitive): --key serves generic CLI-level filtering for any vertex; lens kwargs passthrough serves lens-specific domain vocabulary (--context, --severity, --for-task) that doesn't generalize. Both lands.
design/guidance-as-lens-not-kind                                    mid    1   3  2026-05-15  Dissolution finding: 'guidance' is a lens, not a kind. Reading InferioMinion's guidance lens (~/.config/loops/lenses/guidance.py shared 2026-05-15) reveals it composes six EXISTING kinds — principle, guide, pattern, decision, task, thread — into a tabular knowledge-base view with three render shapes (core-loops universal, domain, generic). No new kind is being introduced; 'guidance' is the lens name and the navigation/routing pattern. Confirms dissolution-test: before adding a kind, check whether the use case is render-shape over existing kinds rather than substrate addition. For knowledge-base / runbook / threaded-skills patterns: the answer is lens composition, not kind invention. This dissolves the kind-introduction question that opened the InferioMinion thread — there is no guidance-kind to design. The substrate is already adequate; what was missing is access primitives (--key, lens kwargs passthrough, possibly --match) so the lens-as-interface contract is complete. Implication for paradigm: 'lens is the interface' (design/lens-is-the-interface) has a substrate-side complement — when a use case feels like it wants a new kind, check first whether it's a new lens over existing kinds. Most knowledge-organization patterns will be lens-shape, not kind-shape.
paradigm/vouch-loops-vocabulary-as-sibling-layers                   mid    1   3  2026-05-16  Meta-pattern recognized 2026-05-15 across three vocabulary walks (scope/potential, delegation/delegate, credential/Grant): vouch terms and loops terms are not competing vocabularies — they are sibling applications of the same structural primitives at different layers. Wire layer and substrate layer share STRUCTURES (Grant, narrowing-delegation, etc.), differ in VOCABULARY (action-shaped vs kind-shaped), are linked by identity (observer-name appears at both) but NOT derived from each other. The dissolution is to recognize and SEPARATE, not to merge. Discriminator for future collisions: 'is this the same operation at a different layer, or two different operations sharing a name?' If different layers: distinguish, name the layer-pair, no translation function. If same operation, same layer, same vocabulary: merge. The over-merge failure mode produces translation machinery (e.g., the audience unpacker proposed then dissolved this session) that has no purpose because the layers don't need to map. Shape: Grant is a structural primitive (horizon + potential); has wire-instance (action-vocab) and substrate-instance (kind-vocab); both are real, neither is canonical. Recurring evidence from this session's walks; apply to future loops/vouch design questions and similar substrate-vs-application vocabulary collisions.

design/vertex-splice-strategy                                       mid    1   3  2026-05-17  Phase 0 grounding outcome for plan:vertex-living-document. STRATEGY: surgical line-based splice, extending the existing kdl_insert_with_row pattern in libs/lang/src/lang/population.py — NOT a greenfield AST→KDL serializer. Pure-canonical re-emit rejected: 36 live vertex files use line comments (//) pervasively; canonical re-emit would lose every comment. CORPUS CHARACTERISTICS (36 live .vertex files surveyed across ~/.config/loops, .loops, meta-discussion, apps): line comments only (no block /* */, no triple-quoted, no escaped quotes); standard KDL constructs (bare-arg nodes, property syntax key=value, multi-arg nodes, block-child nodes, nested blocks); inconsistent indentation between hand-written files (2 vs 4 spaces) — must preserve, not canonicalize; one inline semicolon-separated multi-statement seen (autoresearch.vertex:36 "items collect 50; n count"); numeric args (collect 0/20/50); glob patterns in strings; scope "observer" maps to VertexFile.observer_scoped (one usage: identity); run "..." child nodes on boundaries (two usages). AST COVERAGE: comprehensive — every observed construct maps to an AST node (VertexFile + LoopDef + FoldOp + Boundary + CombineEntry + ObserverDecl + LensDecl + SourcesBlock + TemplateSource). Only lossy field: comments — which surgical splice preserves by design. EXISTING SPLICE PATTERN: kdl_insert_with_row uses splitlines + brace-depth tracking via _find_template_block to locate spans, _detect_indent for indentation, line insertion/removal. 8 tests. Generalizes cleanly to other block types (loops, combine, observers, sources) and other child shapes (kind declarations, vertex entries, observer entries). PHASE 1 SCOPE (revised down): generalize _find_template_block into kdl_find_block(text, path: list[str]); add kdl_insert_child(text, parent_path, child_text) and kdl_remove_child(text, parent_path, child_name, child_key?); reuse _detect_indent. Round-trip tests: parse-then-write should be byte-identical for all 36 corpus files (no-op edit). Mutation tests: insert/remove a kind block, observer, combine entry — verify parseable result + expected AST shape. ~100-150 LOC + tests, not a greenfield serializer. TEST CORPUS: the 36 live .vertex files themselves (no synthetic fixtures needed).

design/tick-chain-at-store-layer                                    mid    1   3  2026-06-09  Tick hash-chaining lives at the STORE layer, not the Tick atom (Kyle's call 2026-06-09, recommended option). Three columns on ticks table: prev_hash (sha256 of previous tick row's canonical bytes — chains the sequence), fact_cursor (max fact ULID at tick time — explicit id-based window boundary, not ts-inferred), window_hash (sha256 over canonical fact rows in (prev_cursor, cursor] in id order — makes FACTS tamper-evident, the actual prize). Rationale: a chain is a property of the persisted sequence, not the snapshot; Tick atom stays pure, no API/serialization change; merge honestly breaks chains (new custody context = correct semantics). Dissolution: delta 1 of the provenance arc requires NO substrate/atom change — pure store-layer property. Precedents followed: pre-chain rows stay NULL (era marker, uuid4-wedge posture); first chained tick's window starts at migration-time max id (epoch marker, no false coverage claims); canonicalization = sorted-compact JSON in one documented helper, NOT JCS — chain needs determinism not interop; JCS stays pinned for federation-facing manifests (delta 2+). Verification walks ticks recomputing both hashes; facts after last tick are the honest uncovered live edge.

design/attestation-envelope-read-path                               mid    1   3  2026-06-10  Attestation envelope surfaces via two existing homes, no new command. (1) verify -v: verify_chain gains include_ticks returning per-tick detail (era, sig validity, window fact count, cursor deref) — data the walk already computes, now kept instead of discarded. (2) TickWindow gains attestation fields (chained, signed, fact_cursor, cursor_kind, cursor_preview) filled by StoreReader.ticks_between(with_envelope=True); drill-down header renders them. Combined/aggregation vertices return empty envelopes — attestation is per-store; an aggregate does not attest.

design/disclosure-vs-domain-query-axis                              mid    1   3  2026-06-14  COHERENCE FINDING reframing rebuild step 3. The design doc (rebuild-design-0.4.0.md §1) assumed loops' --facts/--refs/--diff dissolve into painted Tags gated by ctx.fidelity.shows(). Grounding in fold.py disproves it: all three are DOMAIN-QUERY SELECTORS, not disclosure layers. --diff selects a different fetcher (_build_diff_fetch + trace lens); --facts toggles want_facts (folded vs raw stream); --refs N carries a traversal DEPTH into fetch (painted's store_true Tag can't model the N). painted's Tag model assumes fixed data revealed in named layers; loops' flags change the query itself. So the real dissolution boundary: PURE TERMINAL axes (-q/-v depth, --max-chars/-lines budgets, --plain/--json format, --static/--live/-i mode) dissolve into painted add_cli_args+parse_fidelity; DOMAIN-QUERY selectors (--facts/--diff/--refs) stay loops-side (they parameterize fetch). This follows directly from grow-painted-over-workaround + 'push loops into domain-specific arenas' (Kyle): query selection IS domain, not terminal. Step 3 revised: dissolve the generic terminal flags per view; keep domain flags; merge their loops-computed visibility into the painted-compiled Fidelity.
practice/usage-inverts-the-renderer-thesis                          mid    1   3  2026-06-27  Usage forensics (siftd, 8.5K loops calls, 2026-06-27) inverts the redesign thesis. The dominant consumer of read is an AGENT that wants plain/searchable/sliceable/fact-whole text and REJECTS the styled render: --plain is the single hottest flag in the whole CLI (25.2pct of all calls, 58.1pct of reads), --json near-cold (2.9pct); 67.9-70.2pct of reads are piped through head/grep/tail; 21.8pct of store reads bypass the CLI to raw sqlite. So leverage-the-renderer aimed at the wrong consumer: the styled render is a HUMAN-tier concern, and the human umwelt has ZERO rows in the corpus (unfalsifiable). Static-first = AGENT-CONTRACT-first. Two umwelts: agent (plain+search+fact-whole+budget+projection, measured, dominant) vs human (styled+interactive, unmeasured, judgment+instrument). The interactive tree-drill design is a human-tier second layer we would currently be designing blind. Full report: docs/dev/loops-usage-forensics-2026-06-27.md.

design/salience-three-term-contract                                 mid    1   3  2026-07-02  RATIFIED (Kyle 2026-07-01, from Dissolution View study): the salience contract is the three-term formula salience = f(recency, inbound-refs, digest-coverage). design/internal-row-placement-facts                                 mid    1   3  2026-07-02  RESOLVED (Kyle 2026-07-02): declaration events live in the facts table under a reserved kind namespace (option A). Deciding test = merge must not be lossy about meaning; only fact-residence lets interpretive history travel with the facts it interprets (facts about facts travel as facts). B1 third-table: no shared witness order. B2 chain-rows: chains don't merge, so meaning can't travel. Consequences ratified with it: lineage scoping — genesis event's ULID IS the lineage id; self-resolution folds Latest per (lineage,kind,subject) restricted to self; foreign declarations are inert citizens (carriage is not obligation); merge appends a 'merged' receipt event (source lineage, cursor, dump hash) making native-ontology rewind of imported facts resolvable in one store; native-lineage reads explicit (parallel to unequal cursors); slice preserves lineage id, fork = new genesis via rebirth ceremony. Spec updated: §9.2 Lineage block + merged receipt row, §9.4 resolution recorded.
design/salience-tier-scope-vertex                                   mid    1   3  2026-07-02  RATIFIED (Kyle 2026-07-02): rail tier (◆/│/·) is assigned PER-KEY RELATIVE TO ITS VERTEX, INVARIANT TO VIEW — computed once against the vertex population, same glyph in ls/read/--kind cuts/stream; containers propagate max TIER, so drilling always finds the promised ◆ (scent-trail integrity). Rejected: relative-within-rendered-cut (glyph lies across the drill path — the ◆ followed from ls can vanish in read) and absolute cutoffs (distributions vary wildly per vertex; quiet vertex all-·, hot week all-◆). Same shape as granularity-complete-key-address: the property attaches to the ADDRESS, not the view showing it. Cost accepted: tiers not comparable across vertices (◆ in identity = hot-for-identity) — matches how ls is actually read. ⊘ orthogonal: status overlay stampable over any tier.
design/observer-compound-delegation-path                            mid    1   3  2026-07-04  RATIFIED (Kyle 2026-07-04): 'a/b' observer names read as delegation paths FOR GROUPING ONLY. Confluence nests compounds under their root and rolls the root gutter tier up MAX-over-descendants, but claims no edge — a name-parse has the same epistemic status as an undeclared address-field. When vouch ships endorsement assertions, the read layer joins both: asserted relations render as edges; slash-compounds without a backing assertion render as implied/unendorsed. The slash form is the degenerate inline encoding of the same relation, never migrated away; the gap between implied and endorsed is itself the signal.

design/graph-build1-scope                                           mid    2   2  2026-07-04  AMENDED at build: chain depth cap 32 -> 128. Build finding: with memoized DFS, a cap below real chain length (live chains reach ~60) memo-poisons — nodes first reached past the cap memoize truncated paths, making 'longest' order-dependent. The cycle guard alone guarantees termination; the cap is purely a Python-recursion safety valve, so it must sit ABOVE realistic chain depth, not act as a result bound. Shipped in graph build-1.
